â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Summary\n\n## Overview\nThis document          â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ summarizes the performance optimizations made  â”‚

â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ allocation, tensor operations, and algorithmic â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ improvements.\n\n## Optimizations              â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Applied\n\n### 1. Direct Device Tensor         â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Creation                                       â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ (sampling_batch_info.py)\n**Location**:        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ `python/sglang/srt/sampling/sampling_batch_inâ€¦ â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ = (\n    torch.tensor(\n        ,\n            â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ dtype=torch.float,\n    )\n    .view(-1, 1)\n  â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ .to(device,                                    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ non_blocking=True)\n)\n```\n\n**After**:\n```â€¦ â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ = torch.tensor(\n    ,\n                       â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ dtype=torch.float,\n                           â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ device=device,\n).view(-1,                     â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ 1)\n```\n\n**Impact**: Eliminates unnecessary  â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ CPU-to-GPU memory transfers by creating        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ tensors directly on the target device. This    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ applies to `temperatures`, `top_ps`, `top_ks`, â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ and `min_ps` tensors.\n\n### 2. Optimized      â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Tensor Filling                                 â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ (sampling_batch_info.py)\n**Location**:        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ `python/sglang/srt/sampling/sampling_batch_inâ€¦ â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ torch.dtype(dtype):\n    if lhs is None:\n     â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ lhs = torch.empty((bs1, *shape),               â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ device=device).fill_(default)\n    if rhs is   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ None:\n        rhs = torch.empty((bs2,         â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ *shape),                                       â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ device=device).fill_(default)\n```\n\n**Afterâ€¦ â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ lhs is None:\n    lhs = torch.full((bs1,       â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ *shape), default, dtype=dtype,                 â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ device=device)\nif rhs is None:\n    rhs =     â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ torch.full((bs2, *shape), default,             â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ dtype=dtype,                                   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ device=device)\n```\n\n**Impact**: Uses        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ `torch.full` instead of                        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ `torch.empty().fill_()` which is more          â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ efficient and clearer. Also removes            â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ unnecessary `with torch.dtype(dtype)` context  â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ manager.\n\n### 3. Cached Batch Size           â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Computation                                    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ (sampling_batch_info.py)\n**Location**:        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ `python/sglang/srt/sampling/sampling_batch_inâ€¦ â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ = torch.zeros(\n    len(self.temperatures),\n  â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ self.vocab_size,\n                             â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ ...\n)\n```\n\n**After**:\n```python\nbatch_sâ€¦ â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ = len(self.temperatures)\nself.vocab_mask =    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ torch.zeros(\n    batch_size,\n                â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ self.vocab_size,\n                             â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ ...\n)\n```\n\n**Impact**: Caches the batch    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ size to avoid repeated `len()` calls,          â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ improving readability and potential            â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ performance.\n\n### 4. Optimized List          â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Operations                                     â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ (outlines_backend.py)\n**Location**:           â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ `python/sglang/srt/constrained/outlines_backeâ€¦ â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ (\n    len(jump_forward_bytes) and             â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ jump_forward_bytes[0][0] in                    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ continuation_range\n):\n    byte_edge =        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ jump_forward_bytes.pop(0)\n                    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ suffix_bytes.append(byte_edge[0])\n            â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ cur_state =                                    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ byte_edge[1]\n```\n\n**After**:\n```python\niâ€¦ â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ = 0\nwhile idx < len(jump_forward_bytes) and   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ jump_forward_bytes[0] in continuation_range:\n â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ byte_edge = jump_forward_bytes\n               â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ suffix_bytes.append(byte_edge[0])\n            â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ cur_state = byte_edge[1]\n    idx += 1\n\ndel  â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ jump_forward_bytes[:idx]\n```\n\n**Impact**:   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Replaces O(n) `pop(0)` operations with O(1)    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ indexing, followed by a single O(n) slice      â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ deletion. This is significantly faster for     â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ lists with multiple elements.\n\n### 5.        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Optimized String Formatting                    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ (outlines_backend.py)\n**Location**:           â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ `python/sglang/srt/constrained/outlines_backeâ€¦ â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ = [f"<0x{hex(b)[2:].upper()}>" for b in        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ suffix_bytes]\n```\n\n**After**:\n```python\nâ€¦ â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ = \n```\n\n**Impact**: Uses direct format      â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ specifier `:02X` instead of                    â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ `hex()[2:].upper()`, which is more efficient   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ and cleaner.\n\n### 6. Optimized Loop with zip â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ (xgrammar_backend.py)\n**Location**:           â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ `python/sglang/srt/constrained/xgrammar_backeâ€¦ â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ = 0\nfor i, old_id in                          â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ enumerate(old_output_ids):\n    if old_id ==   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ new_output_ids:\n        k = i + 1\n           â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ else:\n                                        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ break\n```\n\n**After**:\n```python\nk =       â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ 0\nfor old_id, new_id in zip(old_output_ids,   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ new_output_ids):\n    if old_id == new_id:\n   â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ k += 1\n    else:\n                            â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ break\n```\n\n**Impact**: Uses `zip` to        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ iterate over both lists simultaneously,        â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ avoiding manual indexing which is cleaner and  â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ potentially faster.\n\n## Performance          â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Impact\n\nThe optimizations focus on:\n1.      â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ **Memory efficiency**: Direct device           â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ allocation reduces memory copies\n2.           â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ **Computational efficiency**: Better           â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ algorithms (O(1) vs O(n) operations)\n3.       â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ **Code clarity**: Cleaner, more Pythonic code  â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ that\'s easier to maintain\n\n##               â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ Testing\n\nAll optimizations maintain          â”‚
â”‚             â”‚ â”‚ functional equivalence with the original code  â”‚
